""GetSet""classes are used by both view and model classes. In views, they provide the rendered (or user-friendly) value for each of an object's fields. In models, they provide the raw value for each field. If a field is editable by the user, a GetSet class provides ""reverse-translation""between what the user enters and the allowable values and/or data types for a field."
